<span id="freeTextContainer13332183858457434320"><b>5 HUDSON STARS ★★★★★</b> <br/><br/>I can't even begin to tell you how excited I was for this book! I even set an alarm on my iPhone to tell me the book was out so I can get my precious hands on the Kindle edition when it's out (yes I'm an obsessive woman when it comes to Hudson too)<br/><br/>Where do I even start with this review (no worries, spoiler free!) It made me swoon and angry and gooey and frustrated and so many heart-squeezing scenes that I thought I was gonna pass out! Reading from a guy's POV has always been</span>
  <span id="freeText13332183858457434320" style="display:none"><b>5 HUDSON STARS ★★★★★</b> <br /><br />I can't even begin to tell you how excited I was for this book! I even set an alarm on my iPhone to tell me the book was out so I can get my precious hands on the Kindle edition when it's out (yes I'm an obsessive woman when it comes to Hudson too)<br /><br />Where do I even start with this review (no worries, spoiler free!) It made me swoon and angry and gooey and frustrated and so many heart-squeezing scenes that I thought I was gonna pass out! Reading from a guy's POV has always been a different kind of experience, but reading from Hudson's POV? Let me tell you that if I didn't <b>already</b> fall in love with him the first time, I have now <b>
  <u>completely fallen in love with him ten times more</u>
</b>.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>"I can easily divide my life into two parts—before her and after.”</b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Do not be misguided that it's a complete retelling version of the 3 entire books, but rather that this is <b>
  <u>Hudson's story</u>
</b>. It's like the "behind-the-scenes" book of the series, but with even more backstory. AND BOY DID I LEARN SO MUCH. Just when you think you know it all from the earlier series...this one will come from behind and totally hit you with realizations of many, MANY things. <br /><br />When I hit 85% of the book where one of the big scenes played out, I thought I knew how it would play out; the motives, the intentions...but then <b>BAM!</b>. DID LAURELIN PAIGE JUST THREW THAT OUT?! WHAT. OKAY I DID NOT SEE THAT COMING. Seriously people, this book is not what it seems at all! <br /><br />But in all honesty, what drew me in so much to the book was Hudson's reflection of his emotions in the entire book. You can get to see and <b>
  <i>feel</i>
</b> how he dealt with his emotions (or apparently lack thereof in early stages)...all that raw emotions, confusion and what motivated him to do what he did. And his feelings for Alayna, wow..it just moves me from one end to another. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>“This fantasy doesn’t go far though, because of all the decisions I’ve yet to make, there is one thing I know for absolute sure—I can’t tell her how I feel without telling her all of it. My definition of love is still forming, but I am certain it includes transparency and honesty, and I can’t give either without shedding all my secrets.”</b>
</blockquote> <br /><br />SOMEONE JUST RIP MY HEART OUT PLEASE. OH MY POOR HUDSON *heart squeeze*<br /><br />And like the cherry on top of the icing of an amazing book that it is, the book reached perfection with the character or <b>
  <u>Mirabelle.</u>
</b><b>Ladies and gentlemen, someone please get her the MVP trophy award!</b> Just when I thought she was absolutely brilliant in the earlier series, this book will even prove further that she is undoubtedly brilliant and says all the right things! I would like to take all her quotes and keep in a jar and open it up when I need to, so that I can hear her quotes to make me feel loved.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>"Because when you love someone, their world interests you more than your own."</b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Gonna wrap up this review by saying that without a doubt, this book is a <b>
  <u>must-read</u>
</b> especially after reading the earlier series! Definitely re-reading it again because I will need some Hudson-fix. In fact, I even feel like re-reading the entire series. Worth every minute of my life reading Hudson's thoughts and his love for Alayna :) <br /><br />TQ Laurelin for yet another amazing novel and creating a man that stole my heart (again) &lt;3<br /></span>

<div id="review_878019655" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/878019655" />
    <a title="Misha Carlstedt Robinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7352097-misha-carlstedt-robinson"><img alt="Misha Carlstedt Robinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1560369602p2/7352097.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/878019655?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Misha Carlstedt Robinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Misha Carlstedt Robinson" href="/user/show/7352097-misha-carlstedt-robinson">Misha Carlstedt Robinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/21417911-hudson">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer878019655" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17343428587928273350">Hudson was not only a wonderful continuation to the Fixed series, but it was Laurelin Paige's best book to date for me. This was definitely not simply a retelling of the first three books from Hudson's perspective. This book stood on its own as fresh and unique. It gave so much incredible insight into Hudson's past and his motivations, actions, and feelings when it came to Alayna. Through alternating chapters of his life before and after meeting her, this story chronicled Hudson's amazing transf</span>
  <span id="freeText17343428587928273350" style="display:none">Hudson was not only a wonderful continuation to the Fixed series, but it was Laurelin Paige's best book to date for me. This was definitely not simply a retelling of the first three books from Hudson's perspective. This book stood on its own as fresh and unique. It gave so much incredible insight into Hudson's past and his motivations, actions, and feelings when it came to Alayna. Through alternating chapters of his life before and after meeting her, this story chronicled Hudson's amazing transformation from an emotionless master manipulator to a man who willingly gave all of himself to the woman he couldn't live without.<br /><br />As much as I enjoyed Alayna and Hudson's story from Alayna's perspective, there was always more that I wanted to know about Hudson, his youth, and especially his relationship with Celia. I had my moments of frustration with him in the first three books, but it was always minor. In this book I honestly didn't like him at all for much of the first half. There were several times when I wanted to punch him in the face. The depths of the games he played and the way he manipulated people was mind-blowing. It was also insanely fascinating. I have never read a book with a hero like him, and I found myself constantly intrigued by the way his mind worked. Add in his family's dynamics and his relationship with Celia, and the way he changed and grew as the story progressed was especially astounding.<br /><br />Despite my feelings early in the book, it didn't take very long for me to fall right back in love with Hudson. Deep down he was a good man, and Alayna opened up a whole new world for him. It was so easy to see how much he loved her and how much he was willing to sacrifice for her. Hudson had to quite a journey to get to his happily ever after with Alayna, and Paige did a phenomenal job of adding many complex layers to his character. His feelings were so palpable, and even in those moments when I wasn't his biggest fan I truly enjoyed being in his head. In the end he proved just how worthy he was of Alayna's love. This book was an engaging and thought-provoking ride in Hudson's head, and I loved every minute of it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17343428587928273350" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_878574793" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/878574793" />
    <a title="Dali" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2209138-dali"><img alt="Dali" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1407260301p2/2209138.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/878574793?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dali" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dali" href="/user/show/2209138-dali">Dali</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer878574793" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6165105539782876844">There are always two sides to every story, and this is Hudson's and his difficult path towards self-fulfillment.<br/><blockquote>
  <i>“I begin and end with her… Our worlds have entwined and wrapped around each other’s completely. They’ve shaped into something new and fixed and whole. There is no longer her story or mine, but now and always, only ours.”</i>
</blockquote><br/>It’s a common misconception to think that you know a story because you’ve read it. That if you already know what’s going to happen you won’t enjoy it as much as the</span>
  <span id="freeText6165105539782876844" style="display:none">There are always two sides to every story, and this is Hudson's and his difficult path towards self-fulfillment.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I begin and end with her… Our worlds have entwined and wrapped around each other’s completely. They’ve shaped into something new and fixed and whole. There is no longer her story or mine, but now and always, only ours.”</i>
</blockquote><br />It’s a common misconception to think that you know a story because you’ve read it. That if you already know what’s going to happen you won’t enjoy it as much as the first time, or even be bored by it. But Laurelin successfully conveyed this book with a completely different angle making it fresh and new. She takes back in time in between present events. Getting to know H from an early age and how he relates with his family and only friend Celia. Helping us understand him and the motivations to his actions. <br /><br />I was completely engrossed in the story of a broken and mangled man’s psyche and how he was put back together.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Her love is the only beacon of hope I’ve encountered in my dark world. I cling to it. I hold it like a lifeline.”</i>
</blockquote><br />If I hadn’t fallen in love with Hudson from reading the Fixed trilogy, I would have with this book. We get to know him better and in an entirely different light. At first he seemed like bored and spoiled rich kid, a narcissist <i>“who didn’t give a shit about anyone or anything.”</i> But the further I read, saw his self-loathing and felt for his struggle to find “more,” the better I understood that his unfeeling “superpower” was a coping mechanism to deal with heartache and mostly he wanted to understand. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I sensed that there was something to life that I was missing. A color adjustment, perhaps. A flavor that I simply hadn’t been introduced to. A sound that hadn’t found its way to my ears. Something…more.”</i>
</blockquote><br />I loved the way he saw Alayna, how he was enamored with her and sought o protect her. How he recognized a kindred spirit in her and loved her from the start even though he hadn’t recognized it. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I recognized that she’d struggled. And yet she’d come out okay. It was beautiful about her, and I wanted to get to know it more. I wanted that for myself.” <br /><br />“Her carriage was so familiar. Strong on the outside, battling demons on the inside—she was, in so many ways, like me.”</i>
</blockquote><br />I also love them together. In remembering Alayna’s efforts from her point of view in the first three books and now in conjunction with H, they’re perfect for each other. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>“We fit together. We fix each other. We make each other whole.”<br /><br />“I’m lost in her and found in her all at once.”</i>
</blockquote><br />This story has the precise amount of passion and desire, sweetness and romance, heartache and drama that absorbed and captivated me and left me unreasonably wanting more. It was brilliant! <br /><br />This book can be read as a standalone as it encompasses the complete Fixed trilogy and you can start out with it if you’re new to the series. But I strongly suggest you read the complete sequence, they are worth it.<br /><br />For more of my reviews and those of my best book buds, and updates <a href="http://tjlovestoread.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Visit our blog</a><br /><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Tjlovestoread/" rel="nofollow noopener">Stalk us on FaceBook</a><br /><a>As well as Twitter</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6165105539782876844" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_890187156" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/890187156" />
    <a title="Liz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1614203-liz"><img alt="Liz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1561341024p2/1614203.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/890187156?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Liz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Liz" href="/user/show/1614203-liz">Liz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer890187156" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10815348863178797572"><b>5 amazing, you will not be able to put this down, Hudson will make you swoon stars!<br/><br/>"I can easily divide my life into two parts—before her and after.”</b><br/><br/>Hudson is the best male POV ever to be told. Hands down the best I have ever read. I fell head over heels for Hudson in the Fixed series, but in this, I fell totally and completely in love with him. <br/><br/>We met Alayna Withers and Hudson Pierce in the Fixed trilogy. For me it was a fresh story to the boy meets girls and falls in love story. Hudson Pierce </span>
  <span id="freeText10815348863178797572" style="display:none"><b>5 amazing, you will not be able to put this down, Hudson will make you swoon stars!<br /><br />"I can easily divide my life into two parts—before her and after.”</b><br /><br />Hudson is the best male POV ever to be told. Hands down the best I have ever read. I fell head over heels for Hudson in the Fixed series, but in this, I fell totally and completely in love with him. <br /><br />We met Alayna Withers and Hudson Pierce in the Fixed trilogy. For me it was a fresh story to the boy meets girls and falls in love story. Hudson Pierce was unlike any other man I had read about and I fell for him from the beginning. I rooted for them even as I cried for them, yelled at them and wanted to throw my eReader to the wall (or murder Celia, if I could).  I ranted and raved, even as I continued on, because I wanted their HEA. <br /><br />As I was reading the trilogy, I kept thinking to myself, I would love to know what he was thinking at this part, or I wondered what drove him to do that. I was enthralled with every action he took, with every word he said and did not say. And then Laurelin Paige told us she was going to do just that, give us Hudson’s POV. Let me tell you, I imagined all sorts of scenarios and feelings and actions I thought Hudson should say and do, but what Laurelin Paige gave us was so much more. <br /><br />Here I must say that some of this are spoilers if you have not read the trilogy, but not for Hudson, as we know most of the story already. I loved the way the story was given to us. His past intertwined with Hudson and Alayna's present. It just made so much sense and gave us a side of Hudson we needed to see and understand. It was not an easy story to tell, but put Hudson in perspective to what he did to Alayna and why he kept it secret for so long. It did not make it right, but it made us see and understand and love him just a little more. <br /><br />Here I must interject on the story of Hudson and Celia. It really was not what I expected, but I somehow understood it. It was a necessary evil and showed Celia in an entire new light. I have so much to say here, but will not spoil it, but cannot wait to talk about it with others. I will say that if Hudson would have taken the time to see who and what Celia was to him, he might have changed a lot sooner than he did. <br /><br />Another side note, there was a part I wanted to fist pump Mirabelle. You will know what part I am talking about when you read it, but I wish I could have really done it! <br /><br />But ultimately for me, it was Hudson’s emerging emotions for Alayna that made this story for me. Being able to see him as he saw her, as he realized what she truly meant to him, what she could be, that just blew me away. I loved, loved when he ultimately realized that he did truly love her and why he did not tell her as soon as he did. It made sense. He knew he had to fix that one lie before he could truly give himself to her. The raw emotions and honesty we saw in his thoughts and in his fight for her were just wow, wow moments that blew me away. <br /><br />And the additional insight we saw in their relationship (that last chapter) and that epilogue, that alone was worth the read. I do not think I could express how much I loved this series and especially Hudson’s POV, but I truly and honestly did. I know I will reread this time and time again, and what better compliment can I give than that. <br /><br />So without a doubt, yes, I would recommend this book and series. Hudson alone is worth it. He will steal your heart away, I know he did mine. <br /><br />Happy reading <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10815348863178797572" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1134517986" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1134517986" />
    <a title="The Junkie&#39;s Fix is Reading (it&#39;s Em)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22629513-the-junkie-s-fix-is-reading-it-s-em"><img alt="The Junkie&#39;s Fix is Reading (it&#39;s Em)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597579964p2/22629513.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1134517986?book_show_action=true">Dec 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="The Junkie&#39;s Fix is Reading (it&#39;s Em)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="The Junkie&#39;s Fix is Reading (it&#39;s Em)" href="/user/show/22629513-the-junkie-s-fix-is-reading-it-s-em">The Junkie&#39;s Fix is Reading (it&#39;s Em)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22629513-the-junkie-s-fix-is-reading-it-s-em?shelf=billionaire-millionaire-romance">billionaire-millionaire-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22629513-the-junkie-s-fix-is-reading-it-s-em?shelf=favorites-highly-reco">favorites-highly-reco</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22629513-the-junkie-s-fix-is-reading-it-s-em?shelf=favorites-swoonworthy-sexy-hero">favorites-swoonworthy-sexy-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1134517986" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2151795468818942094"><b>Precious 5+++ stars! </b> <br/><br/>Before anything else, I'd like to share that <i>
  <b>Fixed Trilogy</b>
</i> is one of my favorite stories of all time. I love it so much that I have re-read it more than three! Yep, more than three times! (And IMO, it's better that FSOG). I still remember, after reading it, I suffered LSS (<i>last song syndrome</i>) with SO EASY by Philip Philips. I keep singing/playing it for like a week. And I have a book hung-over on the ending of <b>Forever With You </b> , wished there will be more. Especially on</span>
  <span id="freeText2151795468818942094" style="display:none"><b>Precious 5+++ stars! </b> <br /><br />Before anything else, I'd like to share that <i>
  <b>Fixed Trilogy</b>
</i> is one of my favorite stories of all time. I love it so much that I have re-read it more than three! Yep, more than three times! (And IMO, it's better that FSOG). I still remember, after reading it, I suffered LSS (<i>last song syndrome</i>) with SO EASY by Philip Philips. I keep singing/playing it for like a week. And I have a book hung-over on the ending of <b>Forever With You </b> , wished there will be more. Especially on Hudson's POV. And I'm so happy that Ms. Paige, granted that wish. But I had fear, that Hudson's POV is a re-telling of the trilogy (and will only impact me little or disappoint me) so I've shelve it for a long time. <br /><br /><br />Honestly, as a much as I love Hudson in the first 3 books, I <b>HATED him</b> on the <i> before </i>. I can't believe he really could be that cruel. But as the story move forward, I started to see the Hudson I love in <i>Fixed</i>. It's so good to be in his mind and to know that he really feel so much for Alayna. Well, Celia - I'm maybe on the minority here, but I didn't hate her as much as I did on the other books. I can't totally fault her and maybe, hopefully, Ms. Paige will write a story for her? (A girl can wish, right?lol). And I love the Epilogue! So much more than the epilogue of Forever with You. I was in tears.<br /><br />My favorite lines:<br /><br />“They tell the story of a man who’s drowning in his love for a woman. Drowning, but he can still breathe fine. The woman’s flawed, but to him, she’s perfect. She makes his head spin. She’s distracting and inspiring. And he’s so enamored with her that every part of him loves for every part of her. It’s a song about being open, about having no barriers. About loving with “all of me” and asking for “all of you” in return.”<br /><br />“God, she’s amazing. She’s everything that I never knew I wanted. I’m addicted to her—she’s my drug and I can’t get enough of my fix. But she’s also just the opposite. She’s my cure. She’s a balm that eases and relieves me. She’s rehabilitation. She’s remedy. She’s reason.” <br /><br /><br /><i>...and many more...</i><br /><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>#highlyrecommended</i>
</b> <br /><br /><br /> <br /><br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="2151795468818942094" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZWp5sFpADKjeXghupHaMBFFYUGBZpCqmbK/sE9gmTMhvzfUbGNR7cdHvlMWR6nUYTzVYiH8HsM8KHSJL0D3tLA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OV/unlR5Yv1loGdMI7FSb7qAUiV3s6xNi7ZxbCo5H7Mz+GI1Fu0VJGoR++cWLatzpO1azVEQNiTtBL80IiK+Vw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

But what Alayna didn\'t figure on is Hudson Pierce, the new owner of the nightclub.
